## Service Order, Delete

Method: DELETE
[https://csd-staging.heanet.ie/api/space/nsas/l3vpn/service-management/service-orders/32604305]
Accept: none, empty!!

### Failure

#### CSD, JSON or XML

In the body, note that it is not formated as either XML nor JSON

if the SO does not exist

```bash
Failed to find service request Id = 32604305
```

If the SO exists, but has been Completed, deployed to the NE/router

```bash
org.hibernate.exception.ConstraintViolationException: could not execute statement
```

#### Script, r.json()

```python
    request_output = {                      # prepare the data to return as output
        'content': r.text,                # response content as str text of serialized JSON
        # 'content': r.json(),                # response content as a Python dictionary
```

suspect we only get the `Expecting value: line 1 column 1 (char 0)` because we are trying to convert to JSON with `r.json()`
